Free Talk

Agreement and Explanation 214

— Yu Ming

It is a matter of course that superiors do not need to seek the consent of their subordinates for their actions. However, sometimes superiors will explain to their subordinates.

A newly famous world figure said: "Authority existed in primitive times. For example, humans force animals to obey their will, causing them to abandon their free lives, without seeking the animals' consent." This statement is thorough. Otherwise, where would we get beef to eat and horses to ride? The same is true for humans towards humans.

The Japanese bishop recently declared that Japan is the angel mentioned in the Bible: "God will use Japan to conquer the white people who have always slaughtered Jews… to liberate the Jews by force and fulfill the old prophecies." This obviously does not seek the consent of the white people, just as the white people who slaughtered the Jews never sought the consent of the Jews. The Japanese masters in China created the "National Crisis" without seeking the consent of the Chinese people. However, it is another matter when some local gentry seek the consent of the Japanese masters and ask them to maintain local security. In short, to freely eat beef, ride horses, etc., one must declare oneself to be the superior and others to be the subordinates, or compare people to animals, or regard oneself as an angel.

However, the most important thing here is "force," not theory. Neither sociological nor Christian theories can produce any authority. Primitive people's authority over animals arose from the invention of bows and arrows. As for theory, it is merely an explanation thought up afterward. The function of this explanation is to create a religious, philosophical, scientific, and global trend-based foundation for one's own authority, so that slaves and cattle are suddenly enlightened to the laws of this world and abandon all dreams of overturning it.

When superiors explain to their subordinates, you, as a subordinate, must not misunderstand this as seeking your consent, because even if you absolutely disagree, they will still do what they want. They have their dreams, and as long as the power of gold, silver, treasures, airplanes, and artillery is still in their hands, their dreams will come true; while your dreams will ultimately remain just dreams. If, by chance, they come true, they will even say that you copied their old animalistic article.

Random Notes on Mountain Living 215

— A Ying

(5) Firewood, Rice, Oil, and Salt

"(Liangxi Manzhi)" contains a story about "scholars praying for leisure," saying that God asked a scholar, "What do you desire?" He replied, "My desires are very small, and I dare not hope for too much, but I only wish that my life would be adequately clothed and fed, and that I could leisurely live among the mountains and streams until the end of my days." God said, "This is the joy of immortals, and you will not get it." What does this fable illustrate? It is that in the Song Dynasty, the dreams of pastoral poets had already been shattered by "life." Therefore, a poem recorded in a Ming Dynasty novel:

Firewood, rice, oil, salt, sauce, vinegar, and tea,

All seven are in other people's homes.

I cannot worry about it at all,

So I will till the bright moon and plant plum blossoms.

In reality, it is already an "occasional" phenomenon, or "self-consolation." Since the bright moon and plum blossoms cannot be eaten, how can one pick up a hoe, and how can people live? The following poem in "(Lianpo Shihua)" is quite interesting:

Books, paintings, zithers, chess, poetry, wine, and flowers,

I have never left them for years.

Now all seven things have changed,

To firewood, rice, oil, salt, sauce, vinegar, and tea.

A leisurely life and careful study are impossible under unstable living conditions. Firewood, rice, oil, salt, sauce, vinegar, and tea, which constantly swirl in your mind, will always hinder your thinking. Such a poem is a good satire of life. In fact, there is no leisurely tune anymore; at least there will be laments such as "The whole family is in the wind, and the clothes for September have not yet been cut." How should we solve this suffering?

(6) Model of Occasional Writing

Yang Xungi of the Ming Dynasty "(Su Tan)" records:

Zhou Boqi often went to Wu to sell his writings.

He had written nearly a thousand articles in his life. Opening the scrolls, from beginning to end, they were all inscriptions for halls or epitaphs for tombs. Even works celebrating birthdays and mourning deaths were interspersed among them. However, Boqi's talent was particularly strong in this area. Every time he wrote an article for someone, he would gain something, often a tael of silver, or at least one or two hundred coins. Boqi always agreed and promised, writing several articles a day without end. The quality of the work depended on the generosity of the patron. However, as soon as Boqi picked up a pen, he could produce an article, writing in neat, small characters, even in cursive, without seeming to tire. Could it be that his talent was particularly suited to this? After his death, not a single original work of his was left. Those who knew him regretted that he had talent but misused it.

I once wrote an "(Occasional Article)," but I have never mentioned someone who devoted all their life's energy to this work, nor do I know of such a person. Recently, after reading "(Su Tan)," I obtained this information, and I feel that I can add something to it. Writers like Tongcun can be said to be experts in occasional writing. Bookstore owners could publish his collection as a "(Model of Occasional Writing)," and in the current time when occasional writing is needed, business will surely flourish.

Miscellaneous Talk (Little Devils) — Xu Maoyong 216

Mr. Shi Heng criticized Arcibašev's "(Sanin)," believing that Sanin was "(not a historical archetype)" but "(entirely the fruit of artistic fantasy, that is, the author's ideal character)." Therefore; and because the author's artistic creative power was weak, "(it resulted in something very exaggerated and very artificial)."

There is some truth to these words. However, we see that no matter what kind of writer, when creating丨丨or should say describing丨丨a typical character, they often cannot avoid exaggeration and artificiality. Even Bazarov or Rudin under Turgenev's pen have a lot of exaggeration and artificiality to make the reader recognize that there is a typical figure of the era. In addition, like Cervantes's "(Don Quixote)," Goncharov's "(Oblomov)," and Lu Xun's "(Ah Q)," if the author does not add a little exaggeration and artificiality to the typical characteristics of their characters, then the character will not become a typical one, because the typical characteristics are usually mixed in with many ordinary qualities. Without exaggeration and artificiality丨丨that is, what is called "(close-up)" in film art丨丨it is not very obvious. In the countryside, we meet and live with many characters with "(Ah Q spirit)" every day, but before Lu Xun's close-up, our understanding of the characteristics of this Ah Q was never as clear as after reading "(The True Story)." Therefore, the reason why Sanin did not become a typical figure of the era is fundamentally because there was no such character in the social position, which I think is not very related to the author's artistic creative power.

In Russian literature, many writers have created typical characters of the era. Like Bazarov, he is "(an out-and-out model of the new era)," containing "(the hope of new production)." But there are also those who reflect the bankruptcy of the old era and appear as typical representatives of weak human nature, such as the Rudin and Oblomov mentioned earlier, and Sollogub's Peredonov in "(Little Devil)."

Peredonov is a middle school teacher. The goal of his life is to become an inspector of schools. Therefore, he was deceived by his cousin Varvara, who said that there was a duchess who was willing to give him the position of inspector of schools if he could marry Varvara. But he demanded to be an inspector of schools first and get married later. Finally, Varvara forged the duchess's letter of appointment, and they got married. However, in the end, someone told him about the scam, and he was so angry that he killed someone. Sollogub not only wrote Peredonov's character very mean and weak, but all the other characters were also ugly. Except for a few beautiful chapters describing the love of a young couple, almost the entire book is a description of the baseness of human nature. The technique is extremely delicate, with a tragic character as the keynote and many comedic elements added. The book was first published in the "(Problems of Life)" magazine in 1905 and gradually gained a lot of praise and scolding. Those who scolded it said that the protagonist Peredonov was actually a portrait of the author Sollogub himself, and determined that Sollogub was such an ugly and mean character. Sollogub responded to this, saying:

"(Indeed, people like to be loved and are willing to show the sublime aspects of their souls. Even in important people, they hope to see the flash of goodness, the ancient so-called (spark of divinity) (L'etincelle devine). If someone makes a true, correct, ambiguous, and ugly portrait for them, they will not believe it and will think: (This is the author talking about himself!))

(However, not so; dear contemporaries, what I wrote in Little Devils is you. Many of the characters inside are people from among you. This novel is a mirror of the aurora, which I carefully polished with great effort. Its surface is smooth and its texture is pure. I have taken great pains to strive for accuracy. No matter what is reflected on it, it will not change in the slightest, and each will return to its original beauty and ugliness.)

Now the new literature is a signpost, but there was indeed a long period when literature was a mirror of life. Perhaps the difference between New Realism and Old Realism lies in this. But next to the signpost, put a few true and correct portraits, pointing to the devils and zombies on the old road, making people disgusted and terrified, and increasing their enthusiasm for the new road. Is such literature still needed now?

"(Little Devils)" does not yet have a Chinese translation. Probably the translators predicted that no one would want to read it, so they didn't translate it丨丨In addition, the current trend of trusting creation and disliking translation is also a reason. However, if such a book comes out, I know that there will definitely be many people who will read it. Why? Because people of the Peredonov type (Peredonovschina) are too many in front of us, and there are already countless people in our literary world alone. If a mirror is made, they themselves will surely look at themselves and feel pity, and others will surely take it as a warning.

Although Wu Jingzi's "(The Scholars)" and Wu Woyao's "(Strange Events Witnessed Over Twenty Years)" had "(weak artistic creative power)," the influence of these books was great. I hope that there are now writers with rich artistic creative power who can write the typical figures of the modern Chinese Little Devil丨丨But many tabloid literary magnates who are interested in slandering individuals, exposing secrets, and have no artistic creative power are not their choice.

Reading Zheng Xie's Poetry 217

— Zhao Jingshen

Zheng Banqiao said in "(Sending Du Transport Officer Lu Gong's Poem)": "(Clear words are quite like Wang Wei, and learn the essence of Du Fu again.)" This can be said to be the same as saying it about himself. We see that his "(Visiting Ren Gong at Fahai Temple)," "(Revisiting Ren Gong with Abbot Qilin)," "(Sitting at Night in the Mountains)," and other poems are like learning from Wang Wei, while poems such as "(Seven Songs)," "(Crying for the Ox Child)," "(Harsh Official)," "(Evil Private Punishment)," "(Returning Home Trip)" are very similar to Du Fu's poems such as "(Writing in Tonggu County)," "(Stone Moat Official)," and "(Farewell Without a Home)." "(Showing Younger Brother Mo in the Office)" says: "(Learning poetry from three people, Lao Man is also included. Du Fu is after, and Ji Dan is before.)" The third sentence can be proof of learning from Du Fu.

Banqiao's poems are mostly written by impulse, without checking; therefore, a good poem often reveals its fox tail. For example, the last sentence of "(White Gate Willow Flowers)": "(Travelers on the road all love me, and it is okay if I get my lover's pity)," and the last sentence of "(Chrysanthemums for Ten Days)": "(Avoid the warm wind and withstand the cool)," both feel stiff and without poetic meaning. The poem "(Yin Bu)" is written with great energy, showing Banqiao's true colors. In "(Fan County Poems)," the second poem, which describes the little boys and girls of Sang Pang, is the best.

Shallow Lake (10) 218

— Written by Joseph Conrad, translated by Shi Heng

Before him the sun rose gradually above the treetops, and the mist lifted a corner. The breeze was cool; the glory shone on the rippled water and appeared on the lake. The woods also revealed the clear and distinct shadows of the morning, becoming clearer, as if they were closer, and the movement of the leaves and the swaying of the branches also seemed to stop suddenly. In the merciless sunlight, the sounds of nature rose, speaking in an incomprehensible language, telling of the dumb sorrow of mankind. Asat's gaze slowly drifted, staring at the rising sun.

"I can't see anything." He said to himself in a voice that could not be heard.

"There was nothing to begin with." The white man said, walking to the corner of the bamboo platform and waving at his boat. A slight shout came from the lake, and the sampan began to fly towards the home of this ghost-like friend.

"If you want to come with me, I can wait for you one morning," the white man said, looking at the water.

"No, Tuan," Asat said softly, "In this room, I will not be able to eat or sleep, but first I must see my way. Now I can't see anything—I can't see anything! There is no light, no peace in the world; only death, the death of countless people. We are sons of the same mother, but I abandoned him to the enemy's hands; but now I want to go back."

He took a breath and continued in that dreamy tone.

"After a while, I will be able to see clearly, and I will be able to fight—to fight. But she is dead, and…now…darkness."

He waved his arms, then let them slide down along his body, and stared at the sun with that immobile face and stone-like eyes. The white man ran to the boat. The oarsmen skillfully ran along the side of the boat, and looked back from their shoulders at the starting point of the weary journey of the day. The captain, wrapped in white cloth on his head, sat gloomily at the stern, gliding his oars on the water. The white man put his arms on the grass roof of the small cabin, looking back at the sparkling ripples stirred up by the boat. When the sampan had not yet left the lake and reached the river mouth, he raised his eyes. Asat still did not move. In the light of the scorching sun, he stood alone; he had ventured into the darkness of a phantom world beyond the light of a cloudless white day. (End)

Business Tips (42)

Distinguishing True and False American Ginseng, by Cheng Lixing 239

American ginseng is produced in America, and its properties nourish yin and reduce fire. It is particularly effective for treating conditions such as deficiency fire toothache, yin deficiency, and consumptive cough. It is divided into two types: hairy and smooth (i.e., with skin and without skin). The skinless type is called "smooth ginseng" or "front ginseng." It is prized for its white color, light weight, loose texture, and fragrant aroma. Its head is round and square, its body is thick, and its tip is thin and pointed (branches vary greatly in size, and 300 branches are considered moderate for consumption). The surface near the head has deep, dense horizontal lines. It has many short, fat, forked branches. Its taste is initially bitter when chewed, but gradually turns sweet after a moment. This is the superior grade. In recent years, American merchants have increasingly filled the market with fake goods, so a type with the skin left on (i.e., hairy ginseng) has become more common. Its texture, shape, properties, and taste are the same as smooth ginseng, but it has an additional layer of deep, wrinkled yellow-gray skin. Because it is difficult to fake, many buyers prefer it.

American ginseng is expensive, costing 80-90 yuan per catty. Fake ginseng has emerged, created by removing the skin from Japanese ginseng through elaborate processes to make its appearance similar to real ginseng. People from a certain country have specifically established factories to manufacture it, hoping to deceive buyers. Unscrupulous Chinese merchants, tempted by its cheap price of only about 10 yuan per catty, sell it to harm their compatriots. The properties of Eastern and Western ginseng are opposite. Eastern ginseng boosts qi and promotes fire, causing dryness of the mouth and a red face, eventually leading to coughing blood and damaging the body. Fake American ginseng is called "fake smooth" or "competing smooth," also known as "horizontal stripes." Its color is dull white with a slight yellow tint. Its texture is hard and solid, its branches are long and thin with no distinction between thick and thin, and it has no short, fat, forked branches. Both ends are flat and bald. Although it has some stripes, they are very sparse and shallow. Its shape is withered, its aroma is sour, its taste is weak and slightly bitter with astringency, and some have a sticky feeling on the tongue. After chewing a few times, it has no taste.

American ginseng slices are even more difficult to distinguish due to being cut into extremely thin pieces. The real ones are finely glutinous and have a chrysanthemum pattern in the center, but they are often mixed with fake slices. Buyers often try to distinguish them by tasting their bitterness, but monks often soak them in quinine or gentian water before cutting, making them bitter, so this is not a reliable way to distinguish them.

More recently, there are also names such as "cut mouth," "broken tail," "large tail," "medium tail," "thin tail," and "American ginseng whiskers," priced around one yuan per tael, deceptively named "eating embryos" to cater to customers looking for cheap deals. Even experts find it difficult to distinguish these types of goods, so buyers should be even more cautious.

Casual Remarks

On Gentlemen - Preface to Qian 240

Whenever one mentions "gentleman," we are reminded of (Flowers in the Mirror). Although it is explicitly presented as (Flowers in the Mirror), it also contains many profound allegorical meanings. However, its description of the (Country of Gentlemen) depicts the so-called (gentlemen) as excessively (humble and yielding). For example, when two people walk towards each other, neither wants to give way first, and they must lean aside to let the other person pass first. The other person also leans aside in the same way, being humble and polite. As a result, a lot of nonsense is spoken, and some even turn around in anger, willing to take a detour. There are also merchants who are willing to give away their goods regardless of their cost... This is clearly a (hypocritical) depiction, which loses the essence of (allegory).

There are also various different interpretations of (gentleman). Generally, it is considered to be the opposite of (petty person). (Conduct must follow propriety, and words and actions must conform to righteousness) is the general (view of a gentleman). However, there is no absolute definition of this (propriety) and this (righteousness). All good words such as loyalty, filial piety, integrity, trustworthiness, fairness, uprightness, amiability, and humility are generally possessed by (gentlemen) and can earn people's respect. However, unfortunately, the behavior of (gentlemen), which has been passed down for thousands of years until today, has been denounced as (man-eating old ethics) and is to be overthrown. However, there are also people who are simultaneously calling for the promotion and preservation of our country's (inherent virtues).

Whether the (old ethics) should be preserved or overthrown is something I have absolutely no preconceived notions about. According to Mr. Wang Jingzhi's interpretation, the so-called (gentleman) of ancient times should be understood as (upper-class person). In his annotation of (The Ospreys) in (Selected Annotations of the Book of Songs), he states: (Gentleman is an aristocratic class, with titles and power, and a very high social status. It is the ideal figure in the minds of women at that time. The interpretation of gentleman as the opposite of petty person is a mistake...). His reason for interpreting it as (upper-class person) (aristocratic class) is that (gentleman) can be interpreted as (son of the monarch).

However, there are also people who interpret (gentleman) as (scoundrel bastard). This must be attributed to Mr. Wei Jiangong's boldness and frankness in the thirty-eighth issue of (Yu Si). I have copied his original text of (Wei Feng Cutting Sandalwood) below:

Original text of the Book of Songs: (They chop the sandalwood, and pile it on the river bank. The river water is clear and rippling. They do not sow, they do not reap, yet whence comes the grain three hundred sheaves? They do not hunt, they do not fish, yet why do we see badgers hanging in your courtyard? Those (gentlemen), they do not eat for nothing!)

Mr. Wei's interpretation: (The sandalwood is chopped bare, the logs are stacked on the riverbank; the river water ripples clearly. They don't farm, they don't till the land, so why do they get 300 shi of grain for nothing? They don't net or hunt, so why do you see foxes, rabbits, sables, and wolves hanging in your yard? Alas! Those (scoundrel bastards) can't eat without side dishes!)

We don't need to criticize his interpretation, just his humorous and satirical writing style is already worthy of appreciation. And the so-called (gentleman) has really suffered enough.

Ruan Ji of the early Jin Dynasty seems to have been a thinker who advocated naturalism. He greatly admired freedom, but the so-called (gentlemen) of that time did not allow him freedom. He despised the hypocritical rites and laws, and the (scholars of rites and laws) hated him like an enemy. Therefore, he could only spend his remaining years with poetry and wine, and vent his sorrow with weeping. The (gentlemen) of that time once disdainfully ridiculed him as a (mad slave). The (scholars of rites and laws) of that time were very arrogant.

However, in the present, whether the (gentleman) refers to (upper-class person) (aristocratic class) or (scoundrel bastard), it is absolutely of no benefit to today's society. This can be asserted. Even if it refers to the so-called (object of petty people) (a legacy of thousands of years), in today's China, where the people are poor and buying is difficult, the economy is bankrupt in the countryside, and the society is full of unemployment, it is at least not necessary.

Therefore, (gentleman), if it is not immediately... [text missing] displayed in the inner tree.

Modern Celebrity Calligraphy and Painting

Mr. Huang Zongxiang's Landscape (Brief Biography)

Huang Liang, styled Zongxiang, is a native of Huating. He is fond of the six methods and is proficient in landscapes and flowers. This work possesses the rustic charm of Shi Tian. Mr. Huang is especially skilled in national martial arts. His spirit is bold and unrestrained, which is fitting for his brush, which is transcendent and washes away the vulgarity of the marketplace.

Moonlight Night - Yuan Zhi 241

(My love! Let me leave you, let me forever...)

Ah, ah! It is already such a desolate autumn moonlit night, why must the violin of that Russian girl across the way still emit such heartbreaking sounds?

I am familiar with this tune, and it is the only tune I am familiar with. However, for five years, I have never sung it once, because it is too stimulating. As soon as it starts, it pulls me back to the most painful place, making me shed a few more futile tears for the past dreams. I once smashed my violin, I once declined a friend who studied music, I was always on guard, afraid of triggering the sound of this tune. Although I cannot erase the musical score engraved in my brain.

Ah, ah! I want to forget, forget that tragic scene. I am afraid to hear, to hear this mournful sound!

You, you young Russian girl, why don't you play the joyful tune you played the night before last, but on this already desolate autumn moonlit night, play such heartbreaking sounds? What sorrow do you have that you must do this? Aren't you afraid of hurting yourself, but you must know that you have unknowingly pulled me back to the most painful past...

(What? Even the epiphyllum doesn't wither so quickly, does it?)

I clearly remember that five years ago, in the X X Middle School campus covered in faint moonlight, I said these words to her for the last time, with tears in my eyes. It had the form of a question, but there was absolutely no sense of questioning. When I spoke, I just hung my head helplessly... I clearly remember that she seemed to want to say something, but suddenly stood up, shook off my hand, and walked straight away... I also clearly remember how she lay prostrate on the back of another chair, how her back was twitching, but when I chased after her, she suddenly stood up again and went back to the dormitory... I also remember how I braved the wind and dew and stood foolishly in the campus until dawn...

What was correct about the reasons she said in her letters and in person? She didn't say she had changed her mind, but said it was for my sake! She said that the short half-year of love had caused me great loss. She said she was afraid that I would exhaust my ambitions for her sake. She said that I had neglected my studies in the past half year, she said that I had alienated comrades and friends in the past half year, she blamed me for forgetting the great responsibility? (Society is in such urgent need of transformation, which is felt by all young people with a brain. We should do our best to shoulder our responsibilities.) This is the language of her letter. She said we can no longer indulge in love. She said she was leaving, and she was leaving me...

She didn't reply to a single word of my letter. In my letter, I said she was too cold. What's wrong with falling in love passionately when we are young? The great responsibility can be shouldered in the future. I swear that I am not a weak-willed youth, and I will never fail her expectations, but I can never give up the right to love immediately... I remember that my letter paper was stained with tears, I wanted to break her determination... Because of this, she didn't reply a single word. The exam was approaching, and the third day was the holiday. But she still ignored me. Is she really leaving? I was so anxious that my head was about to explode. In the classroom, I always kept my eyes on her, but she didn't even look at me. Her face was pale and serious, which made me have to give up.

The music teacher announced the method of the music exam. Everyone sings a song alone. Singing is fine, singing the score is also fine. The eighth in line was her. She walked to the piano, facing me. I lay on the desk and dared not look up; just concentrating on listening to her beautiful singing voice, for the last time, ah, ah, this is the last time!

She sang, and the score she sang, the first sentence stabbed into my heart. I remember the lyrics that match this score are like this:

My love! Let me leave you.

Let me leave you forever!

It's not that my heart is hard, it's really for your sake.

If we continue to entangle, you will have a great sacrifice.

I don't want you to sacrifice for me, it's better to separate from you.

This is my painful proposition, and I ask you to forgive me.

My love! The more I love you, the more I can't help but leave you!

When the aftersound faded away, I raised my head and saw her slightly moist eyes fixed on me, but as soon as they touched my eyes, she suddenly lowered her head and returned to her seat...

This is the scene of my departure from her. For five years, I have never seen her again. Only this sad song remains in my heart as a souvenir. But, I want to gradually forget this song, forget this scene, I am always on guard, not letting it reappear... But tonight, you Russian girl! Why do you let your violin play such a song to touch my hidden pain? On such a desolate autumn moonlit night...

Because he could no longer compete with others, the president stopped his salary and issued an eviction order. In a desperate situation, he returned to his hometown and, recalling his former fame, couldn't help but cry out loud!

He is over twenty years old. He thought his (omnipotent) two feet were no longer effective. But he had to eat, and he needed a job. He had to seek work in all directions, but what skills did he have? Would society tolerate this ignorant person? At this time, he was extremely regretful. He wanted to strive, but he had no way to strive. So the once glorious sports champion (Black-Faced Tiger) the ball player, fell into poverty for the rest of his life!

Power Cannot Be Suppressed - Zao 243

Recently, at the invitation of a friend, I attended a symposium for factory management colleagues. This is a group that studies all issues related to factory management. First, the colleagues present gave their opinions in turn, and then everyone discussed them. The speech given by Mr. Li, who has been a manager for more than ten years, is worth recording. He said: (Brothers have been working as managers for more than ten years. I feel that because of the changes of the times in the past ten years, our methods of managing workers have also changed to suit the times and trends. That is to replace (violent suppression) with (rational guidance). For example, if two workers are fighting in the factory and come to you to tell you, twisted into a ball. Ten years ago, if you put on a very stern face and shouted (both parties are not allowed to fight), and then suppressed them with the words (if you fight again in the future, both of you will be fired at the same time), you could scare away the opinions of the two people. But if it is now, the above method is not applicable. Because their knowledge and understanding have improved. If the two of them argue and come to you to ask you to judge, if you don't use a reasonable method of mediation and only use power to suppress them, not only will you not be able to eliminate their opinions, but they will also think that you are an irrational person and will not obey your command at the same time...)

Indeed, the times are changing day by day. Not only must the methods of managing workers suit the times and trends, but in fact, why shouldn't those who are people's leaders suit the times and trends? In the past, the emperor was the people's leader. The emperor was noble above all else, and his power shook the four directions. In addition, he held the military and political power in his hands. The common people could not even hear the news. He also created the intimidating saying (the monarch wants the minister to die, and the minister has to die) to prevent reactionaries and to suppress them. It was certainly able to be powerful for a while, but in the end it could not resist the changes of the times and the influx of trends and collapsed. In modern times, the people's knowledge has improved, and they have also realized their own mission. At this time, if those who are people's leaders still do not do some practical work that benefits the masses and continue to use power to suppress them indiscriminately, not only will they not gain the people's trust, but their collapse will be imminent.

Because now is the era of (those who follow the people survive) and (those who go against the people perish). Power cannot be suppressed.

Film Supplement

The Disappearance of the US Film Industry's Overseas Market and How to Break Through the Current Crisis 246

— Wang Yan Zhi

In the era of silent films, the overseas market of the US film industry, especially Europe, was very popular. The production costs of each of their films could be recovered domestically, and the income from overseas markets could reach four-tenths of the total income. By the time of sound films, the overseas market gradually disappeared, because different dialects made stagnation an unavoidable phenomenon. The American film industry has exhausted various strategies in order to regain the lost market. For example, hiring famous European actors to make movies in order to appeal to European audiences, making each film in various language versions in addition to English, or establishing photography studios in Europe to produce films that cater to the psychology of Europeans, can be said to have exhausted all the methods that human intelligence can reach. However, as a result, the European territory is still shrinking day by day. The reasons for this, if explained in detail, would be too lengthy. Now, I will only extract the main points and describe them as follows:

In the current situation, Germany, France, England, Italy, and other European countries all have plans to protect their domestic films. Moreover, under the rule of Mussolini, who advocated nationalism, and Hitler, who ruled Germany, American films naturally have to endure extra heavy pressure. In Hitler's anti-Jewish movement, Jewish Americans were driven out of the country, so the American film industry, in which Jews held the reins, had no hope of assistance. Just look! The branch office established by Paramount in Germany in the past has now been closed and returned to the country. To put it bluntly, in the future, American films may no longer have the opportunity to be publicly screened on German screens (during Hitler's rule).

In addition, photography studios and cinemas established in France and England have also closed due to economic failures. In short, at present, the overseas market of the American film industry is only in British colonies and South America, as well as East Asian countries. Therefore, the total overseas income of the American film industry is only one-third of what it used to be.

In terms of the national character of Europeans, not to mention political restrictions, they are definitely unwilling to spend money to watch films spoken in foreign languages. Therefore, the first so-called countermeasure to break through the crisis is to add foreign language versions. However, this is not easy. Each of their films costs at least 8,000 to 15,000 US dollars. Therefore, at this time, they no longer add foreign language versions except for special works.

Secondly, they feel that the overseas market is disappearing and domestic income is decreasing. From a passive perspective, they can only lay off staff and save expenses. This level is quite strict. For example, Paramount Company has implemented an annual reduction of 2 million US dollars in staff salaries. In addition, there are reductions in production costs and shortening of production time. In the past, an ordinary film would take four to five weeks, but now it is shortened to less than three weeks.

In other aspects, for those who are engaged in screen work, if their luck fades slightly, regardless of whether they are past stars, they are all in the ranks of being discarded. On the one hand, they are doing their best to discover and cultivate new stars, because new stars are cheap and their expenses can be saved.

In short, the American film industry is now working hard, desperately, and fighting this crisis. If, unfortunately, this situation continues for a few more years, then their future is hopeless.

My Critique (Sister's Tragedy) 247

— Luo Tao

Previously, this publication carried Li Renjun's rigorous critique of Hu Ping's screenplay and performance in (Sister's Tragedy), focusing on the film's content and ideas. Now, I offer some additional points.

The story of this film itself is too simple and ordinary; moreover, it is quite unrealistic. For example, the (correction of revenge ideology) and the (inspiration of revolutionary will) are precisely contrary to the film's content. The Ying siblings' assassination of young master Wang is purely an individualistic act of revenge. As Mr. Li commented, this method of assassination leads nowhere. How can it be considered a correction? The director did not contribute much to this film, except for an exaggerated depiction of Shanghai when the father and daughter return home at the beginning, foreshadowing their future return.

At the beginning, I didn't think it was very good that Zheng Xiaoqiu, playing the younger brother, climbed a tree to watch something. Firstly, because Xiaoqiu is so fat, and secondly, a younger brother of that age should, according to family customs, be engaged in farming work, not idly climbing trees to play.

Also, I don't quite understand the reason for the daughter going to Shanghai to play with her father. Considering how poor and busy their family is, would they have so much free time and money to play in Shanghai?

Critique of (Sister's Tragedy) 248

— Yi

(Omitted above) The beginning of this story reveals the bankruptcy of the countryside. The subject matter is certainly pleasing, but after the younger brother is arrested, it develops in a distorted way. The gratuitous insertion of a four-way love triangle and the ensuing jealousy also seem too cumbersome. Especially the ending, with the landlord's son being assassinated to complete the play, inevitably falls into a quagmire of fantasy, almost turning this tragedy, filled with grief and indignation, into a comedy.

It is contradictory that the countryside, already squeezed to the point of requesting rent reduction from the landlord, returns disappointed but brings back many foreign cloths from the city. Using this method to explain the causes of the countryside, in order to make the audience understand, is a clumsy move. Also, the subtitles tell us that Mo Xin is a poor boy, so how can his father order the (Accounting Office) to remit four hundred yuan to provide him with reference books? This is also a point that makes us doubtful. In terms of the actors, I think Hu Ping and Wang Mengshi performed the best. There seems to be some change, which is what the theme of the play dictates. Otherwise, the story would be loose and weak. Her face, filled with sorrow and indignation and brimming with murderous intent, is her outstanding feature. From his appearance to his drowning in the river, Wang Mengshi consistently conveyed solemn and genuine emotions. He is the best of the supporting actors. Gong Jianong did not leave us with a special impression because he appeared very little. Wang Xianzai and Wang Weixin performed mediocrely. Gu Meijun's expressions were too forced, Zheng Xiaoqiu's movements lacked realism, and he had virtually no facial expressions.

Trinkets (8) 255

Granny Ye was really anxious. "Where's Yu'er?..." Her cries pierced everyone's hearts like needles. "Where's Yu'er? My Yu'er?"
